This is a unique opportunity for a Senior Legal Counsel who wants to contribute to a responsible and sustainable energy future. Joining TotalEnergies means working in this space with a shared purpose of decarbonizing energy and being a major player in the energy industry of tomorrow. In Denmark, we are the leading oil and gas company working actively on our base business as well as contributing to the country’s energy transition and broadening our portfolio into renewable energy. \n    <br> \n    <br> Collaborating with a team of 8 dedicated colleagues across our Copenhagen and Esbjerg offices, you will be a member of our Danish Legal and TotalEnergies’ global Legal network providing legal support in an international context and in a challenging legal and regulatory environment. Key internal stakeholders are management and leadership teams across Esbjerg and Copenhagen as well as the E&amp;P Legal department in HQ in Paris.\n    <br> \n    <br> We have an engaging and supportive work environment and are passionate about what we do. You will report to the Head of Legal for Denmark.\n    <br> \n    <br> \n    <b>Your responsibilities<\u002Fb>\n    <br> The purpose of this role is to support the legal needs of TotalEnergies’ Danish affiliates and protect our legal and commercial interests in Denmark, thereby contributing to the value optimization and mitigation of risks through excellence in contracting, regulatory, contractual compliance, and governance. \n    <br> \n    <br> The main activities will be to:\n    <ul>\n     <li> Play a proactive part in the energy transition in Denmark, working with stakeholders on Carbon Capture and Storage, and development of initiatives within Renewable Energies.<\u002Fli>\n     <li> Protect TotalEnergies’ interest under the Sole Concession and in DUC as well as under other licenses and JVs. <\u002Fli>\n     <li>Drive timely and commercially oriented legal advice in compliance with applicable law and clients’ needs in relation to:\n      <ul>\n       <li> procurement, vendors and other contracting issues of moderate and high complexity<\u002Fli>\n       <li> projects such as Gorm Reconfiguration, working closely with our commercial and business development team<\u002Fli>\n      <\u002Ful><\u002Fli>\n     <li> Support regarding GDPR and Danish HR law, company law and governance of TotalEnergies’ Danish affiliates.<\u002Fli>\n     <li> Handle highly complex legal projects and cases and prepare legal opinions<\u002Fli>\n     <li> Manage TotalEnergies’ interests and recommend and execute strategy in relation to legal disputes.<\u002Fli>\n    <\u002Ful>\n    <p><br> <b> Want to know more?<\u002Fb><br> For further information, please contact our General Counsel Heidi Helbo at heidi.helbo@totalenergies.com and\u002For Recruitment Partner, Kamilla Godsk at kamilla-godsk.sorensen@totalenergies.com for HR related questions. <div>\n   <p><b>Context and environment<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n   <div>\n    The position as Production Support Engineer in our Integrated Production Optimization Cell (IPOC) is given the authority and autonomy to identify and initiate the required response in collaboration and agreement with the offshore community to avoid escalation and remedy of the situation. Besides the offshore community, where you will have different interfaces with the OIM, Superintendents, CCR operators, you will also have onshore interfaces with Discipline Engineers and Managers.\n    <br> \n    <br> The IPOC is considered as the main interface between the offshore and onshore organization in production and operational matters. Hence the IPOC shall be capable of operating in the space between and bridging the two entities with the objective to support and solve most of all production and operational issues arisen on the installations. Mattes which cannot be solved in the IPOC either due to complexity, magnitude, or timeframe shall be handed over to the Tier 2 organization. \n    <br> The IPOC is a multi-discipline unit that shall be capable of identifying and analyzing upcoming or already arisen issues. In close collaboration with the offshore community, ensure sound response is taken within agreed time frame to ensure the short-term safety and integrity of the installation, as well as meeting the Environmental and Production (Production and Injection) KPIs set forward for the installation in question. \n    <br> \n    <br> In essence you can look forward to: \n    <ul>\n     <li>Facilitate the daily Operation rhythm within the IPO cell. <\u002Fli>\n     <li>Identify, prioritize actions for IPOC members and track progress. <\u002Fli>\n     <li>Ensure that activities affecting the extraction of hydrocarbons have been identified, planned, and coordinated. <\u002Fli>\n     <li>Provide Input for D2D activities e.g., satellite activity prioritization, pigging, inflow test etc. in consideration of the actual situation on the installation. <\u002Fli>\n     <li>Ensure proper review of IOP (Integrated Operation Plan) and that shortfalls are estimated, communicated, and accepted in advance of activity execution<\u002Fli>\n    <\u002Ful>\n   <\u002Fdiv> \n  <\u002Fdiv>\n  <div>\n   <p><b>Candidate profile<\u002Fb><\u002Fp> \n   <div>\n    To be successful in the position, it is ideal to have good interpersonal skills to manage stakeholders and create the professional network within the organization both offshore and onshore. This position calls for you to be organized and structured in order to maintain the overview and prioritize between multiple activities in a hectic environment. However, it is important that you possess a safety mindset as well and the ability to manage emergency situations, which makes communication skills a key in this role.\n    <br> \n    <br> Finally, it is an advantage that you have:\n    <ul>\n     <li> A degree in Marine Engineering, Mechanical\u002FElectrical Engineering. <\u002Fli>\n     <li>Relevant proven experience within “Upstream” Production Operation or Maintenance disciplines can though compensate for formal education.<\u002Fli>\n     <li> Ideally 5 to 10 years’ experience in “Upstream” Operations. <\u002Fli>\n     <li>Participated in or even leaded multidiscipline teams within Production, Maintenance and Subsurface will be preferred.<\u002Fli>\n     <li> Offshore experience will be an advantage.<\u002Fli>\n     <li> English on professional level both in writing and verbally is prerequisite.<\u002Fli>\n    <\u002Ful>\n    <br> \n    <b> Would you like to help shape better energy?<\u002Fb>\n    <br> Send your application as soon as possible, and no later than\n    <b> 30 January<\u002Fb>, as we will be conducting interviews on a continuous basis.
